 The bill allows the central government to take over the Medical Council of India (MCI)
 emsiai doctoron kii chuni hui niamak sanstha he jo medical shiksha or peshewar gatividhiyon ko niyantrit karti he
 The bill has replaced the ordinance that was introduced in January this year
 medical council of india ko saaf suthra or paardarshee banane kii koshish 2010 se hi chal rahi thi
 Ordinance, brought in January, was the sequel
 sarkaar ne do baar emsiai kii jagah ek nai niamak sanstha laane kii koshish kii
 First in 2011 as National Council of Human Resources in Health (NCHRH) and second time in 2017 as National Medical Commission (NMC)
 lekin yah donon hi koshishen fail ho gai thim
 Union Health Minister Harsh Vardhan said that MCI has failed to complete its work properly and is indulging in corruption
 emsiai ko pehali baar 2010 main niyantran main liya gaya tha jab iske adhyaksh kethan desai ko sibiai ne giraftaar kiya tha
 He was accused of taking a bribe of Rs 2 crore to accredit a medical college in Punjab
 2016 main ek sansadeey panel ne emsiai kii kaary paddati kii jaanch kii or paaya ki iske khilaaf shikayaton kii lambhi fehrist he
 Shortcomings such as lack of accountability and transparency in the investigation, non-fulfillment of mandatory responsibilities, corruption, poor regulation in undergraduate and postgraduate education, and weak controls have emerged
 The Board of Governors is appointed by the government
 is board main 12 sadsy honge, jabaki emsiai main 7 sadsy hote the
 New provisions have also been made in the Bill regarding the eligibility of members
 ab board aaf governors main medical doctoron ke alaava 'prashasnic kshamta or anubhav' vaale export bhi shaamil honge
 The Board will be assisted by a Secretary General, appointed by the Central Government
 vah council ke sachivalay kaa pramukh hoga

 jab raashtrapati ne puure medical kshetra ke liye ek niamak sanstha neshnal council of human resorcej in health (NCHRH) kii sthapana kii ghoshnaa kii thi
 It was an initiative to reform the regulatory body to supply skilled professionals
 iske tahat ucch shiksha or swasthya ke liye alag se council banaai jaani thi
 The process gained momentum in 2010 when the president of MCI was arrested and the government appointed a seven-member Board of Governors through an ordinance, taking control of its operations
 shuru main yah yah vyavastha ek saal ke liye thi lekin aage chalakar ise 2013 tak badha diya gaya
 Meanwhile the NCHRH bill was introduced in 2011 for the establishment of a new regulatory body but a parliamentary panel suggested that it should be withdrawn and re-drafted with adequate opinion and resolution of doubts
 haalanki, 2013 main sarkaar paryaapt kanoonee prakriya ke jariye emsiai kii punarsthapana karne main naakaam rahi or emsiai 2018 tak apane puraane swaroop main hi maujuud rahaa
 During this period, new corruption cases came up against the institution, which reached the Supreme Court and two inspection committees were formed to monitor it
 2018 main duusari nirikshan samiti ne yah kehete hue istipha de diya ki emsiai uske nirdeshon kaa paalan nahin karti he

 The state of Jammu and Kashmir gives special rights or special status over other states in India
 bhartiya samvidhan main asthaayee, sankramanakalin or vishesh upabandh sambandhi bhaag 21 kaa anuchhed 370 jawaharlal nehru ke vishesh hastkshep se taiyaar kiya gaya tha

 dhara 306e se bani thi dhara 370us samay kashmir kaa bharat main vilay karne kii sanvaidhanik prakriya puri karne kaa vakt nahin tha
 In view of this situation Gopalaswami Iyengar presented the draft 306-A in the Federal Constituent Assembly, which later became Article 370
 jisaki vajah se jammu-kashmir ko bharat ke anya rajyon se alag adhikaar mili hai
 According to the provisions of section 370, Jammu and Kashmir has got many special rights
 Parliament has the right to make laws regarding defense, foreign affairs and communication about Jammu and Kashmir, but to implement the law related to any other subject, the Center should state Government approval has to be taken
 isi vishesh darze ke kaaran jammu-kashmir rajya par samvidhan kii dhara 356 lagu nahin hoti
 For this reason, the President does not have the authority to dismiss the constitution of the state
 1976 kaa shahari bhoomi kaanoon jammu-kashmir par lagu nahin hota he
 Under section 370, an Indian citizen has the right to buy land anywhere in India except in the states with special rights
 yani bharat ke duusare rajyon ke log jammu-kashmir main jameen nahin kharid sakate hai
 Article 360 of the Constitution of India i
e
 imposing financial emergency in the country does not apply to Jammu and Kashmir
 jammu-kashmir kaa bharat main vilay karnaa zyaada badi zarurat thi or is kaam ko anjaam dene ke liye dhara 370 ke tahat kuch vishesh adhikaar kashmir kii janata ko us samay diye gayi the
 Which make this state different from other states
 ye hai dhara 370 kii khaas batenjammu-kashmir ke nagarikon ke paas dohari naagarikta hoti he
 The national flag of Jammu and Kashmir is different
 yahaan kii vidhansabha kaa kaarykaal 6 varshon kaa hota he jabaki bharat ke anya rajyon kii vidhansabhaon kaa kaarykaal 5 varsh kaa hota he
 Insulting the national flag or national symbols of India is not a crime in Jammu and Kashmir
 yahaan bharat ke ucchtam nyaayalay ke aadesh maanya nahin hote
 The Parliament of India can legislate with respect to Jammu and Kashmir in a very limited area
 jammu-kashmir kii koi mahila yadi bharat ke kisi anya rajya ke vyakti se vivaah kar le to us mahila kii naagarikta samaapt ho jaaegi
 Conversely, if a Kashmiri woman marries someone from Pakistan, she too gets citizenship of Jammu and Kashmir
